SELECT [t].[Id], [t].[Address], [t].[Address2], [t].[Age], [t].[BHK], [t].[BuiltArea], [t].[CarpetArea], [t].[CityId], [t].[Description], [t].[EstPossessionOn], [t].[FloorNo], [t].[FurnishingTypeId], [t].[Gated], [t].[LastUpdatedOn], [t].[LatestUpdatedBy], [t].[MainEntrance], [t].[Maintenance], [t].[Name], [t].[PostedBy], [t].[PostedOn], [t].[Price], [t].[PropertyTypeId], [t].[ReadyToMove], [t].[Security], [t].[SellRent], [t].[TotalFloors], [t].[Id0], [t].[LastUpdatedOn0], [t].[LatestUpdatedBy0], [t].[Name0], [t].[Id1], [t].[Country], [t].[LastUpdatedOn1], [t].[LatestUpdatedBy1], [t].[Name1], [t].[Id2], [t].[LastUpdatedOn2], [t].[LatestUpdatedBy2], [t].[Name2], [p1].[Id], [p1].[ImageUrl], [p1].[IsPrimary], [p1].[LastUpdatedOn], [p1].[LatestUpdatedBy], [p1].[PropertyId], [p1].[PublicId]
FROM (
    SELECT TOP(1) [p].[Id], [p].[Address], [p].[Address2], [p].[Age], [p].[BHK], [p].[BuiltArea], [p].[CarpetArea], [p].[CityId], [p].[Description], [p].[EstPossessionOn], [p].[FloorNo], [p].[FurnishingTypeId], [p].[Gated], [p].[LastUpdatedOn], [p].[LatestUpdatedBy], [p].[MainEntrance], [p].[Maintenance], [p].[Name], [p].[PostedBy], [p].[PostedOn], [p].[Price], [p].[PropertyTypeId], [p].[ReadyToMove], [p].[Security], [p].[SellRent], [p].[TotalFloors], [p0].[Id] AS [Id0], [p0].[LastUpdatedOn] AS [LastUpdatedOn0], [p0].[LatestUpdatedBy] AS [LatestUpdatedBy0], [p0].[Name] AS [Name0], [c].[Id] AS [Id1], [c].[Country], [c].[LastUpdatedOn] AS [LastUpdatedOn1], [c].[LatestUpdatedBy] AS [LatestUpdatedBy1], [c].[Name] AS [Name1], [f].[Id] AS [Id2], [f].[LastUpdatedOn] AS [LastUpdatedOn2], [f].[LatestUpdatedBy] AS [LatestUpdatedBy2], [f].[Name] AS [Name2]
    FROM [Properties] AS [p]
    INNER JOIN [PropertyTypes] AS [p0] ON [p].[PropertyTypeId] = [p0].[Id]
    INNER JOIN [Cities] AS [c] ON [p].[CityId] = [c].[Id]
    INNER JOIN [FurnishingTypes] AS [f] ON [p].[FurnishingTypeId] = [f].[Id]
    WHERE [p].[Id] = @__id_0
) AS [t]
LEFT JOIN [Photos] AS [p1] ON [t].[Id] = [p1].[PropertyId]
ORDER BY [t].[Id], [t].[Id0], [t].[Id1], [t].[Id2]
